			</ul></div><div  class="d_post_content_main">        <div class="p_content  p_content p_content_icon_row1 p_content_nameplate"><div class="save_face_bg_hidden save_face_bg_0"><a class="save_face_card"></a>            </div>        <cc><div id="post_content_62867967885" class="d_post_content j_d_post_content  clearfix">            花9000块学习驾驶证，花20000买一辆破车，花5块钱买一瓶老白干，守在仇人门口。仇人出来的时候。踩死油门，轰然飞撞，人倒在血泊中……淡定地喝着老白干，等待警察来酒精测试。半月后，法院宣判：醉驾撞人，3年。这比故意杀人判死刑合算多了！我看以后谁他妈还敢惹我！都正儿八经的……都给我悠着点，别一天磨磨唧唧的 驾照我有，破车我有，弄你只需要5块钱。就是这么任性。</div><br></cc><br><div class="user-hide-post-down" style="display: none;"></div>        <div class="achievement_medal_section"></div></div>    <a class="l_post_anchor" name="62867967885l"></a><div class="core_reply j_lzl_wrapper hideLzl" style="min-height:380px"></div></div><div class="clear"></div></div><div class="l_post j_l_post l_post_bright  "  data-field='{&quot;author&quot;:{&quot;user_id&quot;:503570759,&quot;user_name&quot;:&quot;\u9893\u5e9f\u4e86\u8c01\u7684\u6e05\u7eaf&quot;,&quot;name_u&quot;:&quot;%E9%A2%93%E5%BA%9F%E4%BA%86%E8%B0%81%E7%9A%84%E6%B8%85%E7%BA%AF&amp;ie=utf-8&quot;,&quot;user_sex&quot;:1,&quot;portrait&quot;:&quot;47e1e9a293e5ba9fe4ba86e8b081e79a84e6b885e7baaf031e&quot;,&quot;is_like&quot;:1,&quot;level_id&quot;:14,&quot;level_name&quot;:&quot;\u4f20\u5947\u679c\u7c89&quot;,&quot;cur_score&quot;:18881,&quot;bawu&quot;:0,&quot;props&quot;:null},&quot;content&quot;:{&quot;post_id&quot;:62868032774,&quot;is_anonym&quot;:false,&quot;open_id&quot;:&quot;tbclient&quot;,&quot;open_type&quot;:&quot;apple&quot;,&quot;date&quot;:&quot;2015-01-11 17:09&quot;,&quot;vote_crypt&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;post_no&quot;:34,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;comment_num&quot;:17,&quot;ptype&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;is_saveface&quot;:false,&quot;props&quot;:null,&quot;post_index&quot;:28,&quot;pb_tpoint&quot;:null}}' >            <div class="user-hide-post-position"></div><div class="d_author">    				<div class="louzhubiaoshi_wrap">
